 bharat satat vikaas lakshya (esadiji) praapt karne ke maamle main peeche he or is suchakank main vah 149 deshon main 110wein sthaan par he jabaki sweden ko sheersh sthaan hasil hua
 It is clear from the index that all countries are facing major challenges in achieving these ambitious goals
 satat vikaas samaadhaan network (esadsen) or bartlsman sticktang ne nayaa satat vikaas suchakank pesh kiya taaki satat vikaas lakshya kii pragati kaa akalan ho sake or uttardaayitv sunishchit ho
 The index collected data from 149 countries to assess where each country stands in terms of the Sustainable Development Goals in 2016
 suchakank main vibhinn deshon ke 17 vaishvik lakshyon ke maamle main unke pradarshan ke aadhaar par ranking pradaan kii gai he jo satat vikaas ke teen ayaamon - aarthik vikaas, saamaajik samavesh or paryaavaran vahniyata - se jude hai
 SDSN Director Geoffrey Sachs said the index helps various countries prioritize the steps to be taken early, and it shows that there are major challenges facing various countries towards achieving sustainable development goals
 suchakank se desh ko lakshya praapt karne ke liye vyaavhaarik maarg talashne main madad mil sakati he
 The comments jo desh lakshyon ko hasil karne ke kareeb hai ve sabase badi arthvyavasthaaen nahin balki apekshaakrit chote or viksit desh hai
 Sweden ranks first in this index, followed by Denmark and Norway at the top three
 (is khabar ko enditivi team ne sampadit nahin kiya he
 It is published directly from the Syndicate feed
 ) The Sustainable Development Solutions Network (SDSN) and Bertelsmann Stiftung introduced the new Sustainable Development Index to assess the progress of the Sustainable Development Goals and ensure accountability
 suchakank ne 149 deshon ke aankadon kaa sangrah kiya taaki iskaa akalan ho sake ki 2016 main har desh satat vikaas lakshya ke maamle main kahaan khadey hai
 The index provides rankings based on their performance in terms of 17 global goals of different countries that are linked to the three dimensions of sustainable development - economic development, social inclusion and environmental sustainability
 esadsen ke nideshak jeffri sacks ne kaha ki suchakank se vibhinn deshon ko jald uthaae jane vaale kadamon kii praathamikta kii pahchaan karne main madad milti he or isse spasht hota he ki vibhinn deshon ke saamne satat vikaas lakshyon ko praapt karne kii disha main pramukh chunautiyaan hai
 The index can help the country find practical ways to achieve the target
 tippaniyan Countries that are close to achieving goals are not the largest economies but relatively small and developed countries
